<!-- #Content -->
<div id="Content">
	<div class="content_wrapper clearfix">

		<!-- .sections_group -->
		<div class="sections_group">
		
			<div class="entry-content" itemprop="mainContentOfPage">
			
				<div class="section mcb-section   " style="padding-top:50px; padding-bottom:50px; background-color:"><div class="section_wrapper mcb-section-inner"><div class="wrap mcb-wrap one  valign-top clearfix" style=""><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-0px"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><h3>Our <b>Roots </b>curriculum systematically covers all learning areas guided by ECDA’s Curriculum framework yet takes into consideration the children’s natural interests which we will then weave into our lesson plan.</h3>

<h3>Our lessons are activity-based, integrated and developmentally appropriate.</h3>

<h3>Lessons are regularly evaluated and improved.</h3>

<h3> Find out more about our <b>Roots and Wings</b> curriculum <a href="https://bprk.sg/roots-and-wings-programme/">here</a>.</h3></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="section mcb-section equal-height-wrap no-margin-h no-margin-v " style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; background-color:"><div class="section_wrapper mcb-section-inner"><div class="wrap mcb-wrap one-second  valign-top clearfix" style="padding: 60px 3% 50px; background-color: rgb(133, 61, 181); background-image: url(&quot;https://themes.muffingroup.com/be/toy/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/home_toy_wrap_bg.png&quot;); background-repeat: no-repeat; background-position: center center; height: 832.375px;"><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><a name="pre-nursery"></a>
<h2 style="color: #ffffff;">Pre-Nursery</h2></div></div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 20px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_image "><div class="image_frame image_item no_link scale-with-grid aligncenter no_border"><div class="image_wrapper"><img alt="6F478C2E-51E9-40FD-94A6-91BD7035D73A_1_105_c" width="535" height="600" data-src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/6F478C2E-51E9-40FD-94A6-91BD7035D73A_1_105_c.jpeg" class="scale-with-grid ls-is-cached lazyloaded" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/6F478C2E-51E9-40FD-94A6-91BD7035D73A_1_105_c.jpeg"><noscript><img class="scale-with-grid" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/6F478C2E-51E9-40FD-94A6-91BD7035D73A_1_105_c.jpeg" alt="6F478C2E-51E9-40FD-94A6-91BD7035D73A_1_105_c" width="535" height="600" /></noscript></div></div>
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 30px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><p style="color:white;font-weight:bold;">In preparation for ownership of learning at a later age, children are taught independence using mainly skill-based activities.</p>

<p style="color:white;font-weight:bold;">
Many lessons are planned to improve motor skills, social cohesiveness and effectiveness and to enhance their language of communication.</p>

<p style="color:white;font-weight:bold;">As part of the pre-writing preparation, activities such as dough play, scissors skills are features in the learning corners that the young children can look forward to.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="wrap mcb-wrap one-second  valign-top clearfix" style="padding: 60px 3% 50px; background-color: rgb(255, 230, 23); background-image: url(&quot;https://themes.muffingroup.com/be/toy/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/home_toy_wrap_bg.png&quot;); background-repeat: no-repeat; background-position: center center; height: 832.375px;"><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><a name="nursery"></a>
<h2>Nursery</h2></div></div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 20px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_image "><div class="image_frame image_item no_link scale-with-grid aligncenter no_border"><div class="image_wrapper"><img alt="" data-src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/IMG_4031-scaled.jpg" class="scale-with-grid ls-is-cached lazyloaded" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/IMG_4031-scaled.jpg"><noscript><img class="scale-with-grid" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/IMG_4031-scaled.jpg" alt=""   /></noscript></div></div>
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 30px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><p style="font-weight:bold;">Phonics, the tool for reading where the letters of the Alphabet is introduced systemically, is taught.</p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;">Basic Mathematics concepts forms the bulk of Numeracy learning.</p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;">Pre-writing skills continue to be featured here.</p>
</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="section mcb-section equal-height-wrap no-margin-h no-margin-v " style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; background-color:"><div class="section_wrapper mcb-section-inner"><div class="wrap mcb-wrap one-second  valign-top clearfix" style="padding: 60px 3% 50px; background-color: rgb(244, 115, 0); background-image: url(&quot;https://themes.muffingroup.com/be/toy/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/home_toy_wrap_bg.png&quot;); background-repeat: no-repeat; background-position: center center; height: 835.375px;"><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><a name="k1"></a>
<h2 style="color: #ffffff;">Kindergarten 1 (K1)</h2></div></div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 20px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_image "><div class="image_frame image_item no_link scale-with-grid aligncenter no_border"><div class="image_wrapper"><img alt="A7E39FDE-9B0B-4CC9-AA82-5A2D9CEEE860_1_105_c" width="1066" height="600" data-src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/A7E39FDE-9B0B-4CC9-AA82-5A2D9CEEE860_1_105_c.jpeg" class="scale-with-grid ls-is-cached lazyloaded" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/A7E39FDE-9B0B-4CC9-AA82-5A2D9CEEE860_1_105_c.jpeg"><noscript><img class="scale-with-grid" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/A7E39FDE-9B0B-4CC9-AA82-5A2D9CEEE860_1_105_c.jpeg" alt="A7E39FDE-9B0B-4CC9-AA82-5A2D9CEEE860_1_105_c" width="1066" height="600" /></noscript></div></div>
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 30px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><p style="color: #ffffff;font-weight:bold;">Children are guided to independent reading using phonics.</p>

<p style="color: #ffffff;font-weight:bold;">They write using invented spelling and together with their teachers and parents, each milestone of spelling is celebrated.</p>

<p style="color: #ffffff;font-weight:bold;">Academic learning is balanced with gross motor skills development; outdoor and indoor activity times are planned and provided for.</p>

</div></div></div></div><div class="wrap mcb-wrap one-second  valign-top clearfix" style="padding: 60px 3% 50px; background-color: rgb(38, 174, 11); background-image: url(&quot;https://themes.muffingroup.com/be/toy/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/home_toy_wrap_bg.png&quot;); background-repeat: no-repeat; background-position: center center; height: 835.375px;"><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><a name="k2"></a>
<h2 style="color: #ffffff;">Kindergarten 2 (K2)</h2></div></div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 20px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_image "><div class="image_frame image_item no_link scale-with-grid aligncenter no_border"><div class="image_wrapper"><img alt="1E825886-716F-4609-AAB8-F6C2E4E656F0_1_105_c" width="450" height="600" data-src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/1E825886-716F-4609-AAB8-F6C2E4E656F0_1_105_c.jpeg" class="scale-with-grid ls-is-cached lazyloaded" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/1E825886-716F-4609-AAB8-F6C2E4E656F0_1_105_c.jpeg"><noscript><img class="scale-with-grid" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/1E825886-716F-4609-AAB8-F6C2E4E656F0_1_105_c.jpeg" alt="1E825886-716F-4609-AAB8-F6C2E4E656F0_1_105_c" width="450" height="600" /></noscript></div></div>
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 30px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><p style="color: #ffffff;font-weight:bold;">This is where the final layer of foundation is laid.</p>

<p style="color: #ffffff;font-weight:bold;">More abstract learning takes place; fine and gross motors skills are practiced and matured.</p>

<p style="color: #ffffff;font-weight:bold;">Pro-social and language skills are acquired to put children in a good stead for formal school.</p>
</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="section mcb-section equal-height-wrap no-margin-h no-margin-v " style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; background-color:"><div class="section_wrapper mcb-section-inner"><div class="wrap mcb-wrap three-fifth  valign-top clearfix" style="padding: 60px 3% 50px; background-color: rgb(18, 162, 229); background-image: url(&quot;https://themes.muffingroup.com/be/toy/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/home_toy_wrap_bg.png&quot;); background-repeat: no-repeat; background-position: center center; height: 859.328px;"><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><a name="roots&amp;wings"></a>
<h2>Roots &amp; Wings </h2></div></div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 20px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_image "><div class="image_frame image_item no_link scale-with-grid aligncenter no_border"><div class="image_wrapper"><img alt="CIMG8582" width="800" height="600" data-src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/CIMG8582.jpg" class="scale-with-grid lazyload" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw=="><noscript><img class="scale-with-grid" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/CIMG8582.jpg" alt="CIMG8582" width="800" height="600" /></noscript></div></div>
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 30px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix align_justify" style=""><p style="font-weight:bold;">Our new Roots and Wings Programme is available for Kindergarten 1 and Kindergarten 2.</p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;">It is thoughtfully designed to extend children’s learning by providing them with opportunities to apply what they have learnt in the classroom. </p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;">It completes children’s learning cycle and seals knowledge where knowledge learnt is knowledge applied. </p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;"> Call us for more info about our new programme, or find out more <a href="https://bprk.sg/roots-and-wings-programme/">here</a>.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="wrap mcb-wrap two-fifth  valign-middle clearfix" style="padding: 60px 3% 50px; background-color: rgb(255, 0, 119); background-image: url(&quot;https://themes.muffingroup.com/be/toy/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/home_toy_wrap_bg.png&quot;); background-repeat: no-repeat; background-position: center center; height: 859.328px;"><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_image "><div class="image_frame image_item no_link scale-with-grid aligncenter no_border"><div class="image_wrapper"><img alt="CIMG4545" width="450" height="600" data-src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/CIMG4545.jpg" class="scale-with-grid lazyload" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw=="><noscript><img class="scale-with-grid" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/CIMG4545.jpg" alt="CIMG4545" width="450" height="600" /></noscript></div></div>
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 20px;">
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_divider "><hr class="no_line" style="margin: 0 auto 30px;">
</div></div></div></div></div><div class="section mcb-section   " style="padding-top:20px; padding-bottom:0px; background-color:"><div class="section_wrapper mcb-section-inner"><div class="wrap mcb-wrap one  valign-top clearfix" style=""><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix" style=""><h3> <b>Roots</b> focuses on the ECDA learning goals, but in our special 6 hour <b>Roots and Wings Programme</b>, students will use the most current approach - Inquiry Based Learning -  to apply the fundamentals learnt in the<b> Roots </b>session during the additional <b>Wings</b> session. </h3></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="section mcb-section   " style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; background-color:"><div class="section_wrapper mcb-section-inner"><div class="wrap mcb-wrap one  valign-top clearfix" style=""><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_image "><div class="image_frame image_item no_link scale-with-grid no_border"><div class="image_wrapper"><img alt="Roots and wings diagram" width="1067" height="600" data-src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Roots-and-wings-diagram.jpg" class="scale-with-grid lazyload" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw=="><noscript><img class="scale-with-grid" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Roots-and-wings-diagram.jpg" alt="Roots and wings diagram" width="1067" height="600" /></noscript></div></div>
</div><div class="column mcb-column one column_image "><div class="image_frame image_item no_link scale-with-grid no_border"><div class="image_wrapper"><img alt="Roots and wings diagram 2" width="1067" height="600" data-src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Roots-and-wings-diagram-2.jpg" class="scale-with-grid lazyload" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw=="><noscript><img class="scale-with-grid" src="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/Roots-and-wings-diagram-2.jpg" alt="Roots and wings diagram 2" width="1067" height="600" /></noscript></div></div>
</div></div></div></div></div><div class="section mcb-section   " style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; background-color:"><div class="section_wrapper mcb-section-inner"><div class="wrap mcb-wrap one  valign-top clearfix" style=""><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix" style=""><h3> Children learn that the basis of learning is a curious mind that questions, questions and questions!</h3>
<h3>Within Roots &amp;Wings programme, art and music enrichment is included, as well as Sportball and Chinese poetry lessons.</h3></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="section mcb-section   " style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; background-color:"><div class="section_wrapper mcb-section-inner"><div class="wrap mcb-wrap one  valign-top clearfix" style=""><div class="mcb-wrap-inner"><div class="column mcb-column one column_column  column-margin-"><div class="column_attr clearfix" style=""><h2><u>Roots and Wings Gallery</u></h2></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="section the_content has_content"><div class="section_wrapper"><div class="the_content_wrapper"><p><a data-elementor-open-lightbox="yes" data-elementor-lightbox-slideshow="2798ef6" data-elementor-lightbox-title="String4" e-action-hash="#elementor-action%3Aaction%3Dlightbox%26settings%3DeyJpZCI6MjgzNSwidXJsIjoiaHR0cHM6XC9cL2Jwcmsuc2dcL3dwLWNvbnRlbnRcL3VwbG9hZHNcLzIwMTlcLzAyXC9TdHJpbmc0LmpwZyIsInNsaWRlc2hvdyI6IjI3OThlZjYifQ%3D%3D" href="https://bprk.sg/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/String4.jpg"></a></p>
